msg:First there was Ramada, then there was Optics Valley shopping district

When I came to Wuhan in 2005, Optics Valley was still a concept and undeveloped, but Ramada was already a landmark building in the business district.

When I come to Wuhan, I still trust the brand of the old hotel, and there are also surprises

environment:

The status of the hotel boss in Optics Valley is unquestionable. The decoration more than 10 years ago has been very luxurious and advanced, and it is still stable and unconventional.

I booked a double bed room and got a [free] upgraded suite. The room was very large and fully functional. The details of the room are very well done and the experience is particularly good.

facility:

There are several restaurants in the hotel and the environment is very good. Bars and gyms are all available. It should be planned according to foreign-related hotels.

health:

Although the room is large, every corner is thoroughly cleaned, and the public areas are also spotless.

Serve:

From reservation to check-in, room upgrade to return visit after check-out, I was very satisfied.

It is the first choice for business trips, large conferences, family travel, etc.
